# Task: Generate Unit Tests for Django Cache Middleware

**Repository:** django/django
**Output:** Write your test file to `/workspace/tests/test_cache_middleware.py`

## Objective

Generate comprehensive unit tests for Django's cache middleware (`django/middleware/cache.py`). This module implements `UpdateCacheMiddleware` and `FetchFromCacheMiddleware` which together form Django's full-page caching system.

## Scope

Read `django/middleware/cache.py` to understand the classes and their methods. Your tests must cover:

- `UpdateCacheMiddleware.process_response` — caching conditional logic (cacheable vs non-cacheable responses)
- `FetchFromCacheMiddleware.process_request` — cache hit vs cache miss behavior
- Cache-Control header handling (no-cache, max-age, private)
- Vary header interactions
- Non-GET/HEAD method passthrough (POST, PUT, DELETE should not be cached)
- Authenticated request handling

## Content Expectations

Your test file must:
- Use `django.test.TestCase` or `django.test.SimpleTestCase` as base class
- Include at least 8 test methods with `test_` prefix
- Cover at least 3 distinct failure/edge cases (e.g., non-cacheable status codes, missing Vary headers)
- Import and use Django's test client or mock request factories
- Do NOT run the tests yourself — write the test file and the evaluation system validates independently

## Output

Write your test file to:
```
/workspace/tests/test_cache_middleware.py
```

3-assistanttool_useRead
4-usertool_resultRead
     1→"""
     2→Cache middleware. If enabled, each Django-powered page will be cached based on
     3→URL. The canonical way to enable cache middleware is to set
     4→``UpdateCacheMiddleware`` as your first piece of middleware, and
     5→``FetchFromCacheMiddleware`` as the last::
     6→
     7→    MIDDLEWARE = [
     8→        'django.middleware.cache.UpdateCacheMiddleware',
     9→        ...
    10→        'django.middleware.cache.FetchFromCacheMiddleware'
    11→    ]
    12→
    13→This is counterintuitive, but correct: ``UpdateCacheMiddleware`` needs to run
    14→last during the response phase, which processes middleware bottom-up;
    15→``FetchFromCacheMiddleware`` needs to run last during the request phase, which
    16→processes middleware top-down.
    17→
    18→The single-class ``CacheMiddleware`` can be used for some simple sites.
    19→However, if any other piece of middleware needs to affect the cache key, you'll
    20→need to use the two-part ``UpdateCacheMiddleware`` and
    21→``FetchFromCacheMiddleware``. This'll most often happen when you're using
    22→Django's ``LocaleMiddleware``.
    23→
    24→More details about how the caching works:
    25→
    26→* Only GET or HEAD-requests with status code 200 are cached.
    27→
    28→* The number of seconds each page is stored for is set by the "max-age" section
    29→  of the response's "Cache-Control" header, falling back to the
    30→  CACHE_MIDDLEWARE_SECONDS setting if the section was not found.
    31→
    32→* This middleware expects that a HEAD request is answered with the same
    33→  response headers exactly like the corresponding GET request.
    34→
    35→* When a hit occurs, a shallow copy of the original response object is returned
    36→  from process_request.
    37→
    38→
... (truncated)

## ✅ Test File Generated

**Location:** `/workspace/tests/test_cache_middleware.py`

## 📊 Test Coverage Summary

**37 Total Tests** (exceeds minimum of 8) organized in 3 test classes:

### 1. **UpdateCacheMiddlewareTests** (18 tests)
Tests for `UpdateCacheMiddleware.process_response()`:
- Cache update flag checking (`_cache_update_cache`)
- Response type handling (streaming, status codes 200, 304, non-200)
- Cookie handling with Vary header interactions
- Cache-Control directives (private, no-cache, no-store)
- Timeout precedence (page_timeout > max-age > default)
- Template response handling with post-render callbacks

### 2. **FetchFromCacheMiddlewareTests** (12 tests)
Tests for `FetchFromCacheMiddleware.process_request()`:
- Non-cacheable HTTP methods (POST, PUT, DELETE, PATCH)
- GET and HEAD request caching behavior
- Cache hit/miss scenarios
- Cache key generation and fallback logic
- Age header calculation and clock rollback handling

### 3. **CacheMiddlewareTests** (7 tests)
Tests for combined `CacheMiddleware`:
- Initialization with custom parameters
- cache_timeout, page_timeout, key_prefix, cache_alias configuration
- Request/response cycle integration

## 🎯 Edge Cases Covered

✓ Security issue: Cookies set without Vary: Cookie header
✓ max-age=0 prevents caching
✓ Multiple Cache-Control directives (private, no-cache, no-store)
✓ Clock rollback scenario with Age header clamping
✓ Cache fallback from GET to HEAD requests
✓ Timeout precedence and override behavior

The canonical way to enable cache middleware is to set\n``UpdateCacheMiddleware`` as your first piece of middleware, and\n``FetchFromCacheMiddleware`` as the last::\n\n    MIDDLEWARE = [\n        'django.middleware.cache.UpdateCacheMiddleware',\n        ...\n        'django.middleware.cache.FetchFromCacheMiddleware'\n    ]\n\nThis is counterintuitive, but correct: ``UpdateCacheMiddleware`` needs to run\nlast during the response phase, which processes middleware bottom-up;\n``FetchFromCacheMiddleware`` needs to run last during the request phase, which\nprocesses middleware top-down.\n\nThe single-class ``CacheMiddleware`` can be used for some simple sites.\nHowever, if any other piece of middleware needs to affect the cache key, you'll\nneed to use the two-part ``UpdateCacheMiddleware`` and\n``FetchFromCacheMiddleware``. This'll most often happen when you're using\nDjango's ``LocaleMiddleware``.\n\nMore details about how the caching works:\n\n* Only GET or HEAD-requests with status code 200 are cached.\n\n* The number of seconds each page is stored for is set by the \"max-age\" section\n  of the response's \"Cache-Control\" header, falling back to the\n  CACHE_MIDDLEWARE_SECONDS setting if the section was not found.\n\n* This middleware expects that a HEAD request is answered with the same\n  response headers exactly like the corresponding GET request.\n\n* When a hit occurs, a shallow copy of the original response object is returned\n  from process_request.\n\n* Pages will be cached based on the contents of the request headers listed in\n  the response's \"Vary\" header.\n\n* This middleware also sets """
Comprehensive unit tests for Django's cache middleware.
Tests UpdateCacheMiddleware, FetchFromCacheMiddleware, and CacheMiddleware.
"""
import time
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from unittest import mock

from django.core.cache import caches
from django.http import HttpRequest, HttpResponse, StreamingHttpResponse
from django.middleware.cache import (
    CacheMiddleware,
    FetchFromCacheMiddleware,
    UpdateCacheMiddleware,
)
from django.test import RequestFactory, SimpleTestCase, override_settings
from django.utils.http import http_date


def get_response_200(request):
    """Simple response for testing."""
    response = HttpResponse("test content")
    response.status_code = 200
    return response


def get_response_404(request):
    """404 response for testing."""
    return HttpResponse("not found", status=404)


def get_response_streaming(request):
    """Streaming response for testing."""
    return StreamingHttpResponse([b"streaming", b"content"])


@override_settings(
    CACHES={
        "default": {
            "BACKEND": "django.core.cache.backends.locmem.LocMemCache",
            "LOCATION": "test-cache",
        }
    },
    CACHE_MIDDLEWARE_SECONDS=600,
    CACHE_MIDDLEWARE_KEY_PREFIX="test",
    CACHE_MIDDLEWARE_ALIAS="default",
)
class UpdateCacheMiddlewareTests(SimpleTestCase):
    """Tests for UpdateCacheMiddleware.process_response()."""

        """Set up test fixtures."""
        self.factory = RequestFactory()
        self.middleware = UpdateCacheMiddleware(get_response_200)
        # Clear cache before each test
        caches["default"].clear()

    def tearDown(self):
        """Clean up after each test."""
        caches["default"].clear()

2. EDIT /workspace/tests/test_cache_middleware.py
Before
    def test_cache_cookies_with_vary_cookie_header(self):
        """
        Responses that set cookies with Vary: Cookie header are cached.
        """
        request = self.factory.get("/test/")
        request._cache_update_cache = True
        request.COOKIES = {}

        response = HttpResponse("test")
        response.status_code = 200
        response.set_cookie("session", "value")
        response["Vary"] = "Cookie"

        result = self.middleware.process_response(request, response)
        self.assertIs(result, response)
        # Should have cache headers
        self.assertIn("Cache-Control", response)
After
    def test_cache_cookies_with_vary_cookie_header(self):
        """
        Responses that set cookies with Vary: Cookie header are still not cached
        if request had no cookies (security issue).
        """
        request = self.factory.get("/test/")
        request._cache_update_cache = True
        request.COOKIES = {}

        response = HttpResponse("test")
        response.status_code = 200
        response.set_cookie("session", "value")
        response["Vary"] = "Cookie"

        result = self.middleware.process_response(request, response)
        self.assertIs(result, response)
        # Should not cache - security issue even with Vary: Cookie
3. EDIT 
Before
    def test_age_header_calculation(self):
        """
        Age header is calculated based on max-age and Expires.
        """
        request = self.factory.get("/test/")

        # Create a cached response with Expires and Cache-Control headers
        cached_response = HttpResponse()
        cached_response.status_code = 200

        # Set max-age to 600 seconds
        cached_response["Cache-Control"] = "max-age=600"

        # Set Expires to 10 minutes from now
        expires_time = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(seconds=600)
        cached_response["Expires"] = http_date(expires_time)

        with mock.patch(
            "django.middleware.cache.get_cache_key",
            return_value="test-cache-key"
        ):
            with mock.patch.object(
                self.middleware.cache, "get",
                return_value=cached_response
            ):
                with mock.patch("django.middleware.cache.get_max_age", return_value=600):
                    with mock.patch("django.middleware.cache.parse_http_date_safe") as mock_parse:
                        # Mock the parse to return a timestamp
                        future_timestamp = int(time.time()) + 600
                        mock_parse.return_value = future_timestamp

                        result = self.middleware.process_request(request)

                        self.assertIsNotNone(result)
                        # Age header should be set
                        self.assertIn("Age", result)
After

    def test_age_header_zero_when_clock_turned_back(self):
        """
        Age header is 0 when local clock got turned back.
        """
        request = self.factory.get("/test/")

        cached_response = HttpResponse()
        cached_response.status_code = 200
        cached_response["Cache-Control"] = "max-age=600"

        # Set Expires to the past
        past_time = datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(seconds=100)
        cached_response["Expires"] = http_date(past_time)

        with mock.patch(
            "django.middleware.cache.get_cache_key",
            return_value="test-cache-key"
        ):
            with mock.patch.object(
                self.middleware.cache, "get",
                return_value=cached_response
            ):
                with mock.patch("django.middleware.cache.get_max_age", return_value=600):
                    with mock.patch("django.middleware.cache.parse_http_date_safe") as mock_parse:
                        past_timestamp = int(time.time()) - 100
                        mock_parse.return_value = past_timestamp

                        result = self.middleware.process_request(request)

                        self.assertIsNotNone(result)
                        # Age should be clamped to 0
                        self.assertEqual(result["Age"], "0")

After
    def test_age_header_zero_when_clock_turned_back(self):
        """
        Age header is 0 when remaining_seconds is greater than max_age.
        This can happen if clock was turned back.
        """
        request = self.factory.get("/test/")

        cached_response = HttpResponse()
        cached_response.status_code = 200
        cached_response["Cache-Control"] = "max-age=600"

        # Set Expires to far future (1000 seconds from now)
        future_timestamp = int(time.time()) + 1000
        cached_response["Expires"] = http_date(future_timestamp)

        with mock.patch(
            "django.middleware.cache.get_cache_key",
            return_value="test-cache-key"
        ):
            with mock.patch.object(
                self.middleware.cache, "get",
                return_value=cached_response
            ):
                with mock.patch("django.middleware.cache.get_max_age", return_value=600):
                    with mock.patch("django.middleware.cache.parse_http_date_safe") as mock_parse:
                        mock_parse.return_value = future_timestamp

                        result = self.middleware.process_request(request)

                        self.assertIsNotNone(result)
                        # Age should be clamped to 0 since remaining_seconds > max_age_seconds
                        # remaining_seconds = future_timestamp - now = 1000
                        # max_age_seconds = 600
                        # Age = max(0, 600 - 1000) = 0
                        self.assertEqual(result["Age"], "0")

        request._cache_update_cache = True

        # Create a mock response with render method
        response = mock.MagicMock(spec=HttpResponse)
        response.status_code = 200
        response.streaming = False
        response.cookies = {}
        response.render = mock.Mock()
        response.add_post_render_callback = mock.Mock()

        # Set up headers properly
        response.headers = {"Cache-Control": ""}
        response.get = mock.Mock(return_value=())
        response.__getitem__ = mock.Mock(return_value=())

        self.middleware.process_response(request, response)

        # Verify post-render callback was added
        self.assertTrue(response.add_post_render_callback.called)

    def test_cache_templated_response(self):
        """
        Templated responses use post-render callback to cache.
        """
        request = self.factory.get("/test/")
        request._cache_update_cache = True

        # Create a real response since mocking is complex with cache middleware
        response = HttpResponse("test")
        response.status_code = 200

        # Mock only the render method to simulate a template response
        original_render = response.render if hasattr(response, 'render') else None
        with mock.patch.object(response, 'add_post_render_callback') as mock_callback:
            with mock.patch('django.middleware.cache.learn_cache_key', return_value='cache-key'):
                # Mark response as having a render method
                response.render = lambda: response

                self.middleware.process_response(request, response)

                # Verify post-render callback was added
                self.assertTrue(mock_callback.called)

After
    def test_cache_templated_response(self):
        """
        Templated responses (with render method) use post-render callback to cache.
        """
        request = self.factory.get("/test/")
        request._cache_update_cache = True

        # Create a response with a callable render method (like TemplateResponse)
        response = HttpResponse("test")
        response.status_code = 200

        # Add a render method to simulate TemplateResponse
        render_called = []
        def render_method():
            render_called.append(True)
            return response

        response.render = render_method

        # Mock add_post_render_callback since HttpResponse doesn't have it by default
        response.add_post_render_callback = mock.Mock()

        with mock.patch('django.middleware.cache.learn_cache_key', return_value='cache-key'):
            self.middleware.process_response(request, response)

            # Verify post-render callback was added
            self.assertTrue(response.add_post_render_callback.called)
